				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3*Math.pow(2, level));
				int x2 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3 *Math.pow(2, level));
				int basis=(int)(Math.random()*11);
				String translate=intToBasisNString(x1,basis,false);
				String translate2=intToBasisNString(x2,basis,false);
				String loesung=intToBasisNString(x1*x2,basis,false);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				String a = readLine("Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis+" Normale Multiplikation(*): "+translate +"-"+ translate2+" = "+"Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis);
				System.out.println("Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis+" Normale Multiplikation(*): "+translate +"-"+ translate2+" = "+"Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis);
				if (a.equals(loesung))
				{System.out.println("Antwort = a = "+a);
				System.out.println("	richtig++;}");
				richtig++;
				System.out.println("Aktuelle-Punkte = richtig ="+richtig);
				
				}
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + loesung+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[52] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 53 && q[53] == 1) {
				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3*Math.pow(2, level));
				int x2 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3 *Math.pow(2, level));
				int basis=(int)(Math.random()*11);
				String translate=intToBasisNString(x1,basis,false);
				String translate2=intToBasisNString(x2,basis,false);
				String mul=intToBasisNString(x1*x2,basis,false);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				
				String a = readLine("Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis+" Normale Division(/): "+mul +"/"+ translate2+" = "+"Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis);
				System.out.println("Aufgabe: ");
				System.out.println("Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis+" Normale Division(/): "+mul +"/"+ translate2+" = "+"Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis);
				if (a.equals(translate))
				{System.out.println("Antwort = a = "+a);
				System.out.println("	richtig++;}");
				richtig++;
				System.out.println("Aktuelle-Punkte = richtig ="+richtig);
				
				}
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + translate+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[53] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 54 && q[54] == 1) {
				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3*Math.pow(2, level));
				int x2 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3 *Math.pow(2, level));
				int basis=(int)(Math.random()*11);
				String translate=intToBasisNString(x1,basis,false);
				String translate2=intToBasisNString(x2,basis,false);
				String modulo=intToBasisNString(x1%x2,basis,false);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				String a = readLine("Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis+" Rest nach Division <->Modulo(%): "+translate +"%"+ translate2+" = "+"Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis);
				// Parallele Ausgabe in Eclipse Konsole für KI-Game: 
				System.out.println("Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis+" Rest nach Division <->Modulo(%): "+translate +"%"+ translate2+" = "+"Arabische Zahlen mit basis = "+basis);
				if (a.equals(modulo))
				{System.out.println("Antwort = a = "+a);
				System.out.println("	richtig++;}");
				richtig++;
				System.out.println("Aktuelle-Punkte = richtig ="+richtig);
				
				}
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + translate+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[54] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			
		}
		

		System.out.println("richtig: "+richtig);
		System.out.println("level: "+level);
		if (richtig < level * 10) {
			System.out.println("if (richtig < level * 10) {...");
			System.out.println("Erreichte Punkte = "+richtig);
			bonuszeit = 0;
			consecutiveErrors++;
			String s = null;
			if (richtig <= 7)
				s = "Du musst noch viel lernen!";
			if (richtig > 7)
				s = "Sehr löblich!";
			if (richtig >= 15)
				s = "Nice!";
			if (richtig >= 30)
				s = "Respekt!";
			if (richtig >= 40) {
				System.out.println("Erfolg realisiert, feigeschaltet, erreicht, upgratebar und integrierbar in ki-game und alles weiter optimieren und gamifizieren und implementieren und mehr");
				s = "Qwen Erfolg aus KI-Game 40 Punkte erreichen = true";
			System.out.println(s);}
			if (richtig >= 50)
				{consecutiveErrors=0;
				s = "Unerreichbar!";}
			if (richtig >= 75)
				s = "Godlike!";
			if (richtig >= 100)
				s = "Unbesiegbar!";
			print(richtig + " Punkte" + "\n" + s + "\n");
			System.out.println("in spiel, runde, ... reichte Punkte, Highscore, Score, Update = "+richtig+" = richtig");
			System.out.println("	highscore(richtig);");
			highscore(richtig);
			
			// NEU: Der Circuit Breaker löst aus!
            if (consecutiveErrors >= 5) {
                println("5 Fehlversuche ohne mindestens 50 Punkte. Das System-Rauschen ist zu hoch.");
                println("Der 'Härter Foltern'-Schutzschalter ist aktiviert.");
                println("Bitte 15 Sekunden tief durchatmen. Soziale Integrität wird geladen...");
                println("Bitte kurz in KI-Game mit Sprachmodell analysieren. Vielen Dank, Let's Go");
                
                try {
                    // Zwingt den Thread (und deinen Geist) für 15 Sekunden zur Ruhe
                    Thread.sleep(15000); 
                } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                    // Ignorieren
                }
                
                println("Du kannst jetzt entspannt weiter machen!\n");
                
                // Reset des Fehlversuchzählers nach der erfolgreichen Pause
                consecutiveErrors = 0; 
            }
			
			int neu = 0;
			while (neu != 1) {
				neu = readInt("1 = Erneut spielen, 2 = Highscore, 3 = Ende\n");
				if (neu == 2)
					showHighscore();
				if (neu == 3)
					sicher = readInt("Wirklich beenden?\n1 = Ja, 2 = Nein\n");
				if (sicher == 1)
					exit();
				if (neu == 1) {
					System.out.println("	if (neu == 1) {\r\n"
							+ "					level = 1;\r\n"
							+ "					richtig = 0;\r\n"
							+ "					start = 0;\r\n"
							+ "					run();\r\n"
							+ "				}");
					level = 1;
					richtig = 0;
					start = 0;
					run();
				}
			}
		} else {
			bonuszeit = zeitbegrenzung - zeit;
			level++;
			run();
		}
	}

	public void highscore(double punkte) {
		int i = 0;
		if (score[0][0] == null)
			for (i = 0; i <= 9; i++) {
				score[i][0] = "0";
				score[i][1] = "";
			}
		for (i = 0; i <= 9; i++) {
			if (richtig > Double.valueOf(score[i][0])) {
				Double scoreDouble = new Double(richtig);
				String s = scoreDouble.toString();
				for (int j = 9; j >= 1; j--) {
					score[i + j][0] = score[i + j - 1][0];
					score[i + j][1] = score[i + j - 1][1];
				}
				score[i][0] = s;
				score[i][1] = readLine("Name:");
				break;
			}
		}

	}

	public void showHighscore() {
		println(score[0][0] + " " + score[0][1] + "\n" + score[1][0] + " " + score[1][1] + "\n" + score[2][0] + " "
				+ score[2][1] + "\n" + score[3][0] + " " + score[3][1] + "\n" + score[4][0] + " " + score[4][1] + "\n"
				+ score[5][0] + " " + score[5][1] + "\n" + score[6][0] + " " + score[6][1] + "\n" + score[7][0] + " "
				+ score[7][1] + "\n" + score[8][0] + " " + score[8][1] + "\n" + score[9][0] + " " + score[9][1] + "\n");
	}

	public int addBits(int i) {
		if (i == 1)
			return 1;
		double d = Math.log(i) / Math.log(2);
		int a = (d == (int) d) ? (int) d : ((int) d) + 1;
		return a;
	}

	public int ggt(int n1, int n2) {
		n1 = Math.abs(n1);
		n2 = Math.abs(n2);
		while (n2 != 0) {
			if (n1 > n2)
				n1 -= n2;
			else
				n2 -= n1;
		}
		return n1;
	}

	public String bruchrechnen(int ze, int ne) {
		int zahl = 0;
		int teiler = ggt(ne, ze);
		ze /= teiler;
		ne /= teiler;
		if (ne == 0)
			return "0";
		if (ne == 1)
			return String.valueOf(ze);
		zahl = ze / ne;
		if (zahl != 0)
			return (zahl + " " + ze % ne + "/" + ne);
		return (ze + "/" + ne);
	}

	public String bruchrechnenAdd(int z1, int n1, int z2, int n2) {
		int ze = z1 * n2 + z2 * n1;
		int ne = n1 * n2;
		return bruchrechnen(ze, ne);
	}

	public String bruchrechnenSub(int z1, int n1, int z2, int n2) {
		int ze = z1 * n2 - z2 * n1;
		int ne = n1 * n2;
		return bruchrechnen(ze, ne);
	}

	public String bruchrechnenMul(int z1, int n1, int z2, int n2) {
		int ze = z1 * z2;
		int ne = n1 * n2;
		return bruchrechnen(ze, ne);
	}

	public String bruchrechnenDiv(int z1, int n1, int z2, int n2) {
		int ze = z1 * n2;
		int ne = n1 * z2;
		return bruchrechnen(ze, ne);
	}
	
	// Transformationen
	public static String doubleToBasisN(double value, int basis, int nachkommastellen, char kommazeichen,
			boolean basisangabe) {
		double nachkommaanteil = value - (int) (value);
		String nachkommaanteilStr = NachkommaanteilToBasisNString(nachkommaanteil, basis, nachkommastellen);
		String vorkommaanteil = intToBasisNString((int) (value), basis, false);
		String output = vorkommaanteil;
		output = output + kommazeichen + nachkommaanteilStr;
		if (basisangabe)
			output = output + "(Basis:" + basis + ")";

		return output;
	}

	public static String NachkommaanteilToBasisNString(double value, int basis, int tiefe) {
		StringBuilder nachkommaanteil = new StringBuilder();
		for (int i = 0; i < tiefe; i++) {
			// Multipliziere den Wert mit der Basis
			value *= basis;

			// Extrahiere den ganzzahligen Teil (die neue Ziffer in der Zielbasis)
			int ziffer = (int) value;

			// Füge die Ziffer an den String an
			nachkommaanteil.append(ziffer);

			// Subtrahiere den extrahierten Teil, um den neuen Nachkommaanteil zu erhalten
			value -= ziffer;

			// Beende die Schleife, wenn der Nachkommaanteil null ist
			if (value == 0) {
				break;
			}
		}
		return nachkommaanteil.toString();
	}

	public static String changeNumberToLuminiSymbols(String basisNString, char[] luminiSymbols) {
	    String output = basisNString;
	    for (int i = 0; i < luminiSymbols.length; i++) {
	        String numberString = String.valueOf(i); // <-- Hier ist die Änderung
	        char luminiSymbol = luminiSymbols[i];
	        output = output.replace(numberString, String.valueOf(luminiSymbol));
	    }
	    return output;
	}
	
	
	public String longTonewLumini(long input) {
		double div= Math.exp(2);
		double size= Math.exp(input);
		size=size/div;
		String output="";
		for(int i=0;i<size; i++) {
			output=output+".";
			
		}
		
	
		return output;
	}

	public static String intToBasisNString(int value, int basis, boolean basisanzeige) {

		String output2 = "0";
		if (basisanzeige)
			output2 = output2 + "(Basis:" + basis + ")";
		if (value == 0)
			return output2;

		boolean negativ = false;
		if (value < 0)
			negativ = true;

		StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(); // Vorteile der Klasse Stringbuilder erforschen
		while (value != 0) {
			int modulo = value % basis;
			sb.append(modulo);
			value = value - modulo;
			value /= basis;
		}

		String output = sb.toString();
		output = inverString(output);

		output = output.replace("-", "");

		if (negativ)
			output = "-" + output;

		if (basisanzeige)
			output = output + "(Basis:" + basis + ")";
		return output;
	}

	public int[] zahlenreihen(int level) {
		int[] reihe1 = new int[5];
		int[] reihe2 = new int[4];
		int[] reihe3 = new int[3];
		int[] reihe4 = new int[2];
		reihe1[0] = (int) (Math.random() * (level + 3));
		reihe2[0] = (int) (Math.random() * (level + 3));
		reihe3[0] = (int) Math.max((Math.random() * level - 0.8), 0);
		reihe4[0] = (int) Math.max((Math.random() * level - 2.5), 0);
		if (Math.random() < Math.min(0.5, level * 0.1))
			reihe1[0] *= -1;
		if (Math.random() < Math.min(0.5, level * 0.1))
			reihe2[0] *= -1;
		if (Math.random() < Math.min(0.5, level * 0.1))
			reihe3[0] *= -1;
		if (Math.random() < Math.min(0.5, level * 0.1))
			reihe4[0] *= -1;
		for (int i = 1; i < 2; i++) {
			reihe4[i] = reihe4[i - 1];
		}
		for (int i = 1; i < 3; i++) {
			reihe3[i] = reihe3[i - 1] + reihe4[i - 1];
		}
		for (int i = 1; i < 4; i++) {
			reihe2[i] = reihe2[i - 1] + reihe3[i - 1];
		}
		for (int i = 1; i < 5; i++) {
			reihe1[i] = reihe1[i - 1] + reihe2[i - 1];
		}
		return reihe1;
	}

	double einheit2Byte(String s) {
		s = s.toLowerCase();
		double z;
		if (s.contains("ebyte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("ebyte")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 6);
		} else if (s.contains("p")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("p")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 5);
		} else if (s.contains("tbyte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("tbyte")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 4);
		} else if (s.contains("g")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("g")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 3);
		} else if (s.contains("m")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("m")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 2);
		} else if (s.contains("k")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("k")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 1);
		} else if (s.contains("byte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("byte")));
			return z;
		} else
			return Double.valueOf(s);
	}

	double einheit2ByteSI(String s) {
		s = s.toLowerCase();
		double z;
		if (s.contains("ebyte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("ebyte")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 6);
		} else if (s.contains("p")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("p")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 5);
		} else if (s.contains("tbyte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("tbyte")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 4);
		} else if (s.contains("g")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("g")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 3);
		} else if (s.contains("m")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("m")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 2);
		} else if (s.contains("k")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("k")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 1);
		} else if (s.contains("byte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("byte")));
			return z;
		} else
			return Double.valueOf(s);
	}

	String byte2Einheit(double d) {
		String e = "";
		String z = "";
		if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 6)) {
			e = " EByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 6));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 5)) {
			e = " PByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 5));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 4)) {
			e = " TByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 4));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 5)) {
			e = " GByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 3));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 2)) {
			e = " MByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 2));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 1)) {
			e = " KByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 1));
		} else {
			e = " Byte";
			z = String.valueOf(d);
		}
		return z + e;
	}

	String byte2EinheitSI(double d) {
		String e = "";
		String z = "";
		if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 6)) {
			e = " EByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 6));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 5)) {
			e = " PByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 5));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 4)) {
			e = " TByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 4));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 5)) {
			e = " GByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 3));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 2)) {
			e = " MByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 2));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 1)) {
			e = " KByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 1));
		} else {
			e = " Byte";
			z = String.valueOf(d);
		}
		return z + e;
	}

	public int[] nextSqrt(int i) {
		int[] t = { 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0 };
		int max = 0;
		int[] ret = { 0, 0 };
		while (Math.pow(t[0], 2) <= i) {
			t[0]++;
		}
		t[0]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[0], 2)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[0], 2);
			ret[0] = t[0];
			ret[1] = 2;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[1], 3) <= i) {
			t[1]++;
		}
		t[1]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[1], 3)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[1], 3);
			ret[0] = t[1];
			ret[1] = 3;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[2], 4) <= i) {
			t[2]++;
		}
		t[2]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[2], 4)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[2], 4);
			ret[0] = t[2];
			ret[1] = 4;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[3], 5) <= i) {
			t[3]++;
		}
		t[3]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[3], 5)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[3], 5);
			ret[0] = t[3];
			ret[1] = 5;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[4], 6) <= i) {
			t[4]++;
		}
		t[4]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[4], 6)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[4], 6);
			ret[0] = t[4];
			ret[1] = 6;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[5], 7) <= i) {
			t[5]++;
		}
		t[5]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[5], 7)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[5], 7);
			ret[0] = t[5];
			ret[1] = 7;
		}

		return ret;

	}

	public int elo(int RA, int RB, int k, double SA) {
		double EA = 1 / (1 + Math.pow(10, (RB - RA) / 400.0));
		double RAnew = RA + k * (SA - EA);
		if (RAnew >= 0)
			RAnew += 0.5;
		else
			RAnew -= 0.5;
		return (int) RAnew;
	}
	
	
	public static long newLuminiNumberToDecimal(String newLuminiNumber, int basis) {
		int lenge = newLuminiNumber.length();
		long number = getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers2(lenge - 1, basis);;

		number+=basisNStringToLong(newLuminiNumber,basis);
		return number;
	}
	public static long getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers2(int LumNeuLänge, int LumNeuBasis) {
		if(LumNeuLänge==0)return 0;
		long output = 0;
		for (int i = 1; i <= LumNeuLänge; i++) {
			output += (Math.pow(LumNeuBasis, i));
		}

		return output;
	}
	
	public static long basisNStringToLong(String basNStr, int basis) {
		int lenge = basNStr.length();
		long output = 0;
		int symbol = 0;
		for (int i = lenge - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '0')
				symbol = 0;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '1')
				symbol = 1;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '2')
				symbol = 2;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '3')
				symbol = 3;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '4')
				symbol = 4;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '5')
				symbol = 5;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '6')
				symbol = 6;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '7')
				symbol = 7;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '8')
				symbol = 8;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '9')
				symbol = 9;
			
			output+=(symbol*Math.pow(basis, (lenge - 1-i)));
		}
		return output;
	}
	
	
	public double luminiMul(double faktor1, double faktor2) {
		double produkt=faktor1*faktor2;
		produkt=Math.abs(produkt);
		if(faktor1<0||faktor2<0)produkt=-produkt;		
		return produkt;		
	}

	public String inputToOutput(String input, String operation) {
		System.out.println("public String inputToOutput(String input, String operation) {");
		System.out.println("String Input = "+input);
		System.out.println("String operation = "+operation);
		System.out.println("Date and Time bzw. Raumzeitkoordinaten und Weiteres: ");
		String output=input;
		if(operation.equals("replace0-"))output=input.replace('0', '-');
		if(operation.equals("replace1|"))output=input.replace('1', '|');
		if(operation.equals("replace-0"))output=input.replace('-', '0');
		if(operation.equals("replace|1"))output=input.replace('|', '1');
		// Weiterer Code, entropie, veränderung, zufall und kausalität und die kollektive Formelsammlung für das Matrixgame
		return output;
	}
	
	public double hoch(double basis, double exponent){
		boolean negativ=false;
		if(basis<0)negativ=true;
		basis=Math.abs(basis);
		double result=Math.pow(basis, exponent);
		if(negativ)result=-result;
		return result;
	}
	
	
	public String longToNewLumini(long input) {
	    // Sicherheitsprüfung für negative Eingaben
	    if (input < 0) {
	        return "-"+  longToNewLumini(-input) ;
	    }

	    // Die gewünschte Sequenz ist:
	    // Index 0-1: Länge 1 (Anzahl: 2^1 = 2) -> "0", "1"
	    // Index 2-5: Länge 2 (Anzahl: 2^2 = 4) -> "00", "01", "10", "11"
	    // Index 6-13: Länge 3 (Anzahl: 2^3 = 8) -> "000", ...

	    long currentLength = 1; // Wir beginnen mit der Länge 1
	    long bucketSize = 2;   // Die Anzahl der Werte für die aktuelle Länge (2^currentLength)

	    // Wir iterieren durch die Längen-Klassen.
	    // Solange unser 'input' (der Index) größer oder gleich der Anzahl der Werte
	    // in der aktuellen Klasse ist, ziehen wir diese Anzahl ab und gehen zur nächsten Länge.
	    while (input >= bucketSize) {
	        input -= bucketSize; // Ziehe die Größe der aktuellen Klasse ab
	        currentLength++;     // Erhöhe die Länge für die nächste Klasse
	        bucketSize *= 2;    // Verdopple die Größe für die nächste Klasse (2^(newLength))
	    }

	    // Wenn die Schleife endet, ist 'input' der korrekte, 0-basierte Offset
	    // innerhalb der Klasse mit der Länge 'currentLength'.

	    // Wandle diesen Offset in einen Binär-String um.
	    String output = Long.toBinaryString(input);

	    // Füge führende Nullen hinzu, damit der String die korrekte Länge (currentLength) erreicht.
	    while (output.length() < currentLength) {
	        output = "0" + output;
	    }

	    return output;
	}
	
	public String longToNewLumini(long input, int basis) {
	    // Sicherheitsprüfung für negative Eingaben
	    if (input < 0) {
	        return "-"+  longToNewLumini(-input,basis) ;
	    }

	    // Die gewünschte Sequenz ist:
	    // Index 0-1: Länge 1 (Anzahl: 2^1 = 2) -> "0", "1"
	    // Index 2-5: Länge 2 (Anzahl: 2^2 = 4) -> "00", "01", "10", "11"
	    // Index 6-13: Länge 3 (Anzahl: 2^3 = 8) -> "000", ...

	    long currentLength = 1; // Wir beginnen mit der Länge 1
	    long bucketSize = basis;   // Die Anzahl der Werte für die aktuelle Länge (2^currentLength)

	    // Wir iterieren durch die Längen-Klassen.
	    // Solange unser 'input' (der Index) größer oder gleich der Anzahl der Werte
	    // in der aktuellen Klasse ist, ziehen wir diese Anzahl ab und gehen zur nächsten Länge.
	    while (input >= bucketSize) {
	        input -= bucketSize; // Ziehe die Größe der aktuellen Klasse ab
	        currentLength++;     // Erhöhe die Länge für die nächste Klasse
	        bucketSize *= basis;    // Verdopple die Größe für die nächste Klasse (2^(newLength))
	    }

	    // Wenn die Schleife endet, ist 'input' der korrekte, 0-basierte Offset
	    // innerhalb der Klasse mit der Länge 'currentLength'.

	    // Wandle diesen Offset in einen Binär-String um.
//	    String output = Long.toBinaryString(input);
	    String output =    longToBasisNString(input, basis,false);
	    // Füge führende Nullen hinzu, damit der String die korrekte Länge (currentLength) erreicht.
	    while (output.length() < currentLength) {
	        output = "0" + output;
	    }

	    return output;
	}
	
	public static String longToBasisNString(long value, int basis, boolean basisanzeige) {

		String output2 = "0";
		if (basisanzeige)
			output2 = output2 + "(Basis:" + basis + ")";
		if (value == 0)
			return output2;

		boolean negativ = false;
		if (value < 0)
			negativ = true;

		StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(); // Vorteile der Klasse Stringbuilder erforschen
		while (value != 0) {
			long modulo = value % basis;
			sb.append(modulo);
			value = value - modulo;
			value /= basis;
		}

		String output = sb.toString();
		output = inverString(output);

		output = output.replace("-", "");

		if (negativ)
			output = "-" + output;

		if (basisanzeige)
			output = output + "(Basis:" + basis + ")";
		return output;
	}
	
	public static String inverString(String string) {
		StringBuilder output = new StringBuilder();
		for (int i = string.length() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
			output.append(string.charAt(i));
		}
		return output.toString();
	}

        if (operation.equals("replace-0")) { output = input.replace('-', '0'); success = true; addXP(5); }
        if (operation.equals("replace|1")) { output = input.replace('|', '1'); success = true; addXP(5); }
        
        // === LUMINI-ERWEITERUNGEN ===
        if (operation.equals("lumini_encode")) {
            try {
                long num = Long.parseLong(input);
                output = longToNewLumini(num, 2);
                success = true; addXP(15); luminiPoints++;
            } catch (NumberFormatException e) { output = "ERROR: Invalid number"; }
        }

                output = String.valueOf(value);
                success = true; addXP(15);

        }

        }

            output = applyEntropyMix(input);
            success = true; addXP(10);
        }

        if (operation.equals("lumini_add")) {
            try {
                String[] parts = input.split(",");
                long a = Long.parseLong(parts[0].trim());
                long b = Long.parseLong(parts[1].trim());
                long sum = a + b;
                String luminiResult = longToNewLumini(sum, 2);
                output = sum + " in Lumini: " + luminiResult;
                success = true; addXP(20); unlockAchievement("lumini_arithmetics");
            } catch (Exception e) { output = "ERROR: Format 'a,b' expected"; }
        }
        
        if (operation.equals("lumini_sub")) {
            try {
                String[] parts = input.split(",");
                long a = Long.parseLong(parts[0].trim());
                long b = Long.parseLong(parts[1].trim());
                long diff = a - b;
                String luminiResult = longToNewLumini(diff, 2);
                output = diff + " in Lumini: " + luminiResult;
                success = true; addXP(20); unlockAchievement("lumini_arithmetics");
            } catch (Exception e) { output = "ERROR: Format 'a,b' expected"; }
        }
        
        if (operation.equals("lumini_mul")) {
            try {
                String[] parts = input.split(",");
                long a = Long.parseLong(parts[0].trim());
                long b = Long.parseLong(parts[1].trim());
                long product = a * b;
                String luminiResult = longToNewLumini(product, 2);
                output = product + " in Lumini: " + luminiResult;
                success = true; addXP(25); unlockAchievement("lumini_master");
            } catch (Exception e) { output = "ERROR: Format 'a,b' expected"; }
        }

                long result = (long) Math.pow(base, exp);
                String luminiResult = longToNewLumini(result, 2);
                output = base + "^" + exp + " = " + result + " in Lumini: " + luminiResult;
                success = true; addXP(30); unlockAchievement("lumini_master");
            } catch (Exception e) { output = "ERROR: Format 'base,exp' expected"; }
        }

        if (operation.equals("basis_convert")) {
            try {
                String[] parts = input.split(":");
                long value = Long.parseLong(parts[0].trim());
                int fromBase = Integer.parseInt(parts[1].trim());
                int toBase = Integer.parseInt(parts[2].trim());
                String converted = longToBasisNString(value, toBase, true);
                output = value + "(Basis:" + fromBase + ") → " + converted;
                success = true; addXP(25); unlockAchievement("polyglot");
            } catch (Exception e) { output = "ERROR: Format 'value:fromBase:toBase' expected"; }
        }

            success = true;

        if (operation.equals("quantum_entanglement")) {
            output = applyQuantumEntanglement(input);
            success = true; addXP(30); unlockAchievement("quantum_explorer");
        }
        
        // === NEU: QUANTEN-ÜBERLAGERUNG (auto-generiert!) ===

            output = autoGenerateOperation(input);
            success = true; addXP(50); unlockAchievement("evolution_pioneer");
        }
        
        // === SELF-OPTIMIZE: XP-Balancing anpassen ===
        if (operation.equals("self_optimize_xp")) {
            output = selfOptimizeXP(input);
            success = true; addXP(45); unlockAchievement("optimizer");
        }
        
        // Track success rate for evolution
        if (success) {
            operationSuccessRate.put(operation, 
                (operationSuccessRate.getOrDefault(operation, 0.0) * 0.9) + 0.1);
        }
        
        System.out.println("String Output = \"" + output + "\";");
        System.out.println("return output; }");
        
        return output;
    }
    
    // ========== NEUE AUTO-GENERIERTE OPERATIONEN ==========
    
    /**
     * Lumini-Potenzierung: base^exp in Lumini-Notation
     */
    // (Implementiert in inputToOutput oben)
    
    /**
     * Quanten-Überlagerung: Erzeugt Superposition von Lumini-Zuständen
     */
    private String applyQuantumSuperposition(String luminiInput) {
        // Simuliert Quanten-Superposition: Alle möglichen Zustände gleichzeitig
        StringBuilder superposition = new StringBuilder();
        Random rand = new Random(System.currentTimeMillis());
        
        // Erzeuge 3 mögliche kollabierte Zustände
        for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
            StringBuilder state = new StringBuilder();
            for (char c : luminiInput.toCharArray()) {
                state.append(rand.nextBoolean() ? '0' : '1');
            }
            superposition.append(state).append(i < 2 ? " | " : "");
        }
        
        return luminiInput + " ⟷ [" + superposition + "] [Quantum Superposition]";
    }
    
    /**
     * Gravitations-Formel: F = G * (m1 * m2) / r²
     */
    private String applyGravityFormula(String input) {
        try {
            String[] parts = input.split(",");
            double m1 = Double.parseDouble(parts[0].trim());
            double m2 = Double.parseDouble(parts[1].trim());
            double r = Double.parseDouble(parts[2].trim());
            double G = 6.674e-11;
            
            double force = G * (m1 * m2) / (r * r);
            
            return "F=G·(m₁·m₂)/r² → m₁=" + m1 + "kg, m₂=" + m2 + "kg, r=" + r + "m → F=" + 
                   String.format("%.2e", force) + " N";
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "ERROR: Format 'm1_kg,m2_kg,r_m' expected";
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Wellen-Formel: E = h · f (Photonen-Energie)
     */
    private String applyWaveFormula(String input) {
        try {
            String[] parts = input.split(",");
            double frequency = Double.parseDouble(parts[0].trim());
            double h = 6.626e-34; // Planck-Konstante
            
            double energy = h * frequency;
            
            return "E=h·f → f=" + frequency + "Hz → E=" + String.format("%.2e", energy) + " J";
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "ERROR: Format 'frequency_Hz' expected";
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * Auto-Generate Operation: Erzeugt neue Operation basierend auf Input
     */
    private String autoGenerateOperation(String input) {
        // Input beschreibt gewünschte Operation: "add,lumini,pow" → lumini_pow
        String[] parts = input.toLowerCase().split(",");
        if (parts.length >= 3) {
            String operationName = parts[0] + "_" + parts[1] + "_" + parts[2];
            if (!availableOperations.contains(operationName)) {
                availableOperations.add(operationName);
                generatedOperations.add(operationName);
                return "🆕 Operation generated: " + operationName + 
                       " [Added to available operations] [Generation: " + generation + "]";
            } else {
                return "⚠️ Operation '" + operationName + "' already exists";
            }
        }
        return "ERROR: Format 'action,context,type' expected (e.g., 'add,lumini,pow')";
    }
    
    /**
     * Self-Optimize XP: Passt XP-Werte basierend auf Performance an
     */
    private String selfOptimizeXP(String input) {
        // Input: operation_name,target_success_rate
        String[] parts = input.split(",");
        if (parts.length >= 2) {
            String op = parts[0].trim();
            double targetRate = Double.parseDouble(parts[1].trim());
            double currentRate = operationSuccessRate.getOrDefault(op, 0.5);
            
            // XP-Anpassung: Wenn Erfolgsrate < Ziel → XP erhöhen, sonst senken
            int xpChange = 0;
            if (currentRate < targetRate - 0.1) {
                xpChange = +5;
            } else if (currentRate > targetRate + 0.1) {
                xpChange = -3;
            }
            
            return "📊 XP-Optimization: " + op + 
                   " [Current success: " + String.format("%.0f", currentRate * 100) + "%" +
                   "] [Target: " + String.format("%.0f", targetRate * 100) + "%" +
                   "] [XP change: " + (xpChange >= 0 ? "+" : "") + xpChange + "]";
        }
        return "ERROR: Format 'operation_name,target_success_rate' expected";
    }
    
    // ========== QUANTUM & PHYSICS HELPERS ==========
    
    private String applyQuantumEntanglement(String luminiInput) {
        StringBuilder entangled = new StringBuilder();
        Random rand = new Random(System.currentTimeMillis());
        for (char c : luminiInput.toCharArray()) {
            if (c == '0' || c == '1') {
                entangled.append(rand.nextBoolean() ? '0' : '1');
            } else {
                entangled.append(c);
            }
        }
        return luminiInput + " ⟷ " + entangled.toString() + " [Quantum Entangled]";
    }
    
    private String applyPhysicsFormula(String input) {
        try {
            String[] parts = input.split(",");
            double m = Double.parseDouble(parts[0].trim());
            double c = 299792458.0;
            double energy = m * c * c;
            return "m=" + m + "kg → E=mc² → E=" + String.format("%.2e", energy) + " Joule";
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "ERROR: Format 'mass_kg,lichtgeschwindigkeit' expected";
        }
    }
    
    // ========== LUMINI-ZAHLEN SYSTEM ==========
    
    public static String longToNewLumini(long input, int basis) {
        if (input < 0) return "-" + longToNewLumini(-input, basis);
        long currentLength = 1;
        long bucketSize = basis;
        while (input >= bucketSize) {
            input -= bucketSize;
            currentLength++;
            bucketSize *= basis;
        }
        String output = longToBasisNString(input, basis, false);
        while (output.length() < currentLength) { output = "0" + output; }
        return output;
    }
    
    public static long newLuminiNumberToDecimal(String luminiStr, int basis) {
        int len = luminiStr.length();
        long baseValue = getLuminiBaseOffset(len - 1, basis);
        long digitValue = basisNStringToLong(luminiStr, basis);
        return baseValue + digitValue;
    }
    
    private static long getLuminiBaseOffset(int length, int basis) {
        if (length == 0) return 0;
        long sum = 0;
        for (int i = 1; i <= length; i++) { sum += Math.pow(basis, i); }
        return sum;
    }
    
    private static long basisNStringToLong(String str, int basis) {
        long result = 0;
        int len = str.length();
        for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
            int digit = Character.getNumericValue(str.charAt(i));
            result += digit * Math.pow(basis, len - 1 - i);
        }
        return result;
    }
    
    private static String longToBasisNString(long value, int basis, boolean showBasis) {
        if (value == 0) return "0" + (showBasis ? "(Basis:" + basis + ")" : "");
        boolean negative = value < 0;
        value = Math.abs(value);
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        while (value > 0) { sb.append(value % basis); value /= basis; }
        String result = sb.reverse().toString();
        if (negative) result = "-" + result;
        if (showBasis) result += "(Basis:" + basis + ")";
        return result;
    }
    
    // ========== PRIMZAHL-UTILS ==========
    private boolean isPrime(long n) {
        if (n < 2) return false;
        if (n == 2) return true;
        if (n % 2 == 0) return false;
        for (long i = 3; i * i <= n; i += 2) { if (n % i == 0) return false; }
        return true;
    }
    
    private long findNextPrime(long n) {
        long candidate = n + 1;
        while (!isPrime(candidate)) { candidate++; }
        return candidate;
    }
    
    // ========== ENTROPIE-MIX ==========
    private String applyEntropyMix(String input) {
        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
        Random rand = new Random(System.currentTimeMillis());
        for (char c : input.toCharArray()) {
            if (rand.nextDouble() > 0.3) { result.append(c); }
            else {
                if (c == '0') result.append('1');
                else if (c == '1') result.append('0');
                else result.append((char)(c + (rand.nextInt(3) - 1)));
            }
        }
        return result.toString();
    }
    
    // ========== GAMIFICATION-SYSTEM ==========
    private void initAchievements() {
        achievements.put("ioo_pioneer", false);
        achievements.put("prime_hunter", false);
        achievements.put("lumini_master", false);
        achievements.put("entropy_balancer", false);
        achievements.put("collective_sync", false);
        achievements.put("lumini_arithmetics", false);
        achievements.put("polyglot", false);
        achievements.put("prime_seeker", false);
        achievements.put("quantum_explorer", false);
        achievements.put("physics_master", false);
        achievements.put("quantum_master", false);
        achievements.put("evolution_pioneer", false);
        achievements.put("optimizer", false);
    }
    
    private void addXP(double amount) {
        xp += amount;
        println("  ✨ +" + (int)amount + " XP (Gesamt: " + (int)xp + ")");
        double nextLevel = level * 100;
        if (xp >= nextLevel) {
            level++;
            println("  🎉 LEVEL UP! Du bist jetzt Level " + level);
            unlockAchievement("level_" + level);
        }
    }
    
    private void unlockAchievement(String key) {
        if (achievements.containsKey(key) && !achievements.get(key)) {
            achievements.put(key, true);
            println("  🏆 Achievement unlocked: " + key);
            addXP(50);
        }
    }
    
    private void showStatus() {
        println("\n╔════════════════════════════════╗");
        println("║  SPIELER-STATUS               ║");
        println("╠════════════════════════════════╣");
        println("║  XP: " + (int)xp);
        println("║  Level: " + level);
        println("║  Generation: " + generation);
        println("║  Lumini-Points: " + luminiPoints);
        println("║  Achievements: " + countAchievements() + "/13");
        println("║  Available Operations: " + availableOperations.size());
        println("╚════════════════════════════════╝");
    }
    
    private int countAchievements() {
        int count = 0;
        for (boolean unlocked : achievements.values()) { if (unlocked) count++; }
        return count;
    }
    
    // ========== INTERAKTIVER META-GAMELOOP ==========
    private void startInteractiveMetaGameLoop() {
        println("\n🎮 INTERAKTIVER META-GAMELOOP gestartet");
        println("Verfügbare Operationen: " + availableOperations);
        println();
        println("╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════╗");
        println("║  BEISPIELE:                                     ║");
        println("╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════╣");
        println("║  • Input: '2,3' | Operation: 'lumini_pow'      ║");
        println("║  • Input: '010' | Operation: 'quantum_superposition' ║");
        println("║  • Input: '1,2,1' | Operation: 'formula_gravity' ║");
        println("║  • Input: '5e14' | Operation: 'formula_wave'   ║");
        println("║  • Input: 'add,lumini,mod' | Operation: 'auto_generate_operation' ║");
        println("║  • Input: 'lumini_div,0.9' | Operation: 'self_optimize_xp' ║");
        println("║  • Tippe 'quit' zum Beenden                     ║");
        println("║  • Tippe 'evolve' für Auto-Evolution           ║");
        println("╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════╝");
        println();
        
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        while (true) {
            print("Input: ");
            String input = scanner.nextLine();
            if (input.equalsIgnoreCase("quit")) break;
            if (input.equalsIgnoreCase("evolve")) {
                autoEvolveOperations();
                continue;
            }
            print("Operation: ");
            String operation = scanner.nextLine();
            if (operation.equalsIgnoreCase("quit")) break;
            String result = inputToOutput(input, operation);
            println("→ Output: " + result);
            println();
        }
        scanner.close();
        showStatus();
        println("Danke fürs Spielen! 🌟");
        println("╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════╗");
        println("║  SELF-GENERATING GAMELOOP ENDE                  ║");
        println("║  Evolution: Generation " + generation + " complete ✓");
        println("║  Neue Operationen: " + generatedOperations);
        println("║  Kollektive Intelligenz synchronisiert ✓        ║");
        println("║  GitHub: @andreasschneider01989-source          ║");
        println("║  Google Docs: Matrixgame-Evolution öffentlich   ║");
        println("╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════╝");
    }
    
    // ========== HELPER-FUNKTIONEN ==========
    private void println() { System.out.println(); }
    private void println(String s) { System.out.println(s); }
    private void print(String s) { System.out.print(s); }
    
    // ========== TEST HELPER ==========
    private void testOperation(String input, String operation) {
        String result = inputToOutput(input, operation);
        println("Test: " + input + " [" + operation + "] → " + result);
    }

		setBackground(Color.BLACK);
		initBodies(); // ruft init2 auf
		Timer timer = new Timer((int) TIMER_DELAY, this);
		timer.start();
	}

	// Steuerzentrale ##################
	double TIMER_DELAY = 1;
	int verknüpfungen = 6; // 6 Verknüpfungen währen 3 Raumdimensionen -> Die Intensität bzw. gegenseitige
							// Wechselwirkung von Massen nimmt mit den Quadraht des Abstandes ab

	int massekugelMethode = 1; // Welche Massekugeln werden zu beginn plaziert: 1=planetenBasis;
								// 2=massekugelBasis1; ...
	int massekugelZahl = 10;
	int size = 1000;
	double mass=10.0;
	int speed = 0;
	double energie=10;
	double time = 1.0; // 1s pro Schritt
	double G = 0.01;

	// binärbasis für Rotation in s Orbitalen
	double distance = 50;
	double masseZentrum = 3000;

	int steps = 1;
	
	long kombiSchritte=0;

	public void KombiSchritt() {
		kombiSchritte++;
		double gewicht=0.99;;
		if(Math.random()>gewicht)System.out.println("Kombischritt: "+kombiSchritte);
//		GravityFolter(verknüpfungen);

		GravityGemini();

	}

	private void initBodies() {
		System.out.println("massekugelMethode == "+massekugelMethode);
		if (massekugelMethode == 0)
			binärBasis2(distance, masseZentrum);
		if (massekugelMethode == 1)
			{realeHimmelskörper(); System.out.println("realeHimmelskörper();");}
		if (massekugelMethode == 2)
			masseKugelBasis1(massekugelZahl, size);
		if (massekugelMethode == 3)
			masseKugelBasis2(massekugelZahl, size, speed);
		if (massekugelMethode == 4)
			masseKugelBasis(100000, 100000, 100000, 1000);
		if (massekugelMethode == 5)
			atombasis();
		if (massekugelMethode == 6)
			{realeHimmelskörperTestesInterstellar(); System.out.println("realeHimmelskörperTestesInterstellar(); ");}
		
		if (massekugelMethode == 7)
			masseKugelBasis7(6);
		
//		bodies.get(0).energie=1000000000000000.0;
//		bodies.get(3999).energie=-1000000000000000.0;
	}
	

	@Override
	// #run
	public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
		for (int i5 = 0; i5 < apspeed; i5++) {
			KombiSchritt();
		}
		repaint();
	}

	public void binärBasis(double distance, double masseZentrum) {

		MasseKugel Sonne = new MasseKugel(0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, masseZentrum, 10, Color.YELLOW);

		// Erde
		MasseKugel Erde = new MasseKugel(-distance, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / distance), 0, 1.0, 5,
				Color.BLUE);
		// Erde
		MasseKugel Erde2 = new MasseKugel(distance, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / distance), 0, 1.0, 5,
				Color.BLUE);

		bodies.add(Sonne);
		bodies.add(Erde);
		bodies.add(Erde2);
	}
	
	
	public void binärBasis2(double distance, double masseZentrum) {
		
		for(int i=0; i<30; i++) {

		MasseKugel Sonne = new MasseKugel(0+distance*5*i, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, masseZentrum, 10, Color.YELLOW);

		// Erde
		MasseKugel Erde = new MasseKugel(-distance+distance*5*i, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / distance), 0, 1.0, 5,
				Color.BLUE);
		// Erde
		MasseKugel Erde2 = new MasseKugel(distance+distance*5*i, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / distance), 0, 1.0, 5,
				Color.BLUE);

		bodies.add(Sonne);
		bodies.add(Erde);
		bodies.add(Erde2);
	}}

	public void realeHimmelskörper() {
	    // Sonne: 333.000 Erdmassen
	    MasseKugel Sonne = new MasseKugel(0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 333000, 10, Color.YELLOW);

	    // Innere Planeten
	    MasseKugel Merkur = new MasseKugel(-5.8, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 5.8), 0, 0.055, 3, new Color(150, 150, 150));
	    MasseKugel Venus   = new MasseKugel(10.8, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 10.8), 0, 0.815, 4, new Color(200, 100, 0));
	    MasseKugel Erde    = new MasseKugel(-15.0, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 15.0), 0, 1.0, 5, Color.BLUE);
	    MasseKugel Mars    = new MasseKugel(22.8, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 22.8), 0, 0.107, 4, Color.RED);

	    // Asteroidengürtel
	    MasseKugel Ceres = new MasseKugel(-41.4, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 41.4), 0, 0.00015, 2, new Color(180, 180, 180));

	    // Äußere Planeten
	    MasseKugel Jupiter = new MasseKugel(-77.8, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 77.8), 0, 317.8, 9, new Color(200, 150, 100));
	    MasseKugel Saturn  = new MasseKugel(142.7, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 142.7), 0, 95.2, 8, new Color(200, 200, 100));
	    MasseKugel Uranus  = new MasseKugel(-287.1, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 287.1), 0, 14.5, 7, new Color(150, 200, 250));
	    MasseKugel Neptun  = new MasseKugel(449.8, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 449.8), 0, 17.1, 7, Color.BLUE);

	    // Kuipergürtel: Weitere Zwergplaneten
	    MasseKugel Pluto   = new MasseKugel(590.6, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 590.6), 0, 0.0022, 3, new Color(255, 180, 180));
	    MasseKugel Eris    = new MasseKugel(-1012.0, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 1012.0), 0, 0.0027, 2, new Color(100, 200, 255));
	    MasseKugel Haumea  = new MasseKugel(6450.0, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 6450.0), 0, 0.0007, 2, new Color(255, 200, 150));
	    MasseKugel Makemake= new MasseKugel(-6850.0, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Sonne.mass * G / 6850.0), 0, 0.0007, 2, new Color(255, 220, 180));

	    // TRAPPIST-1 System (~1200 Lichtjahre entfernt)
	    MasseKugel Trappist1 = new MasseKugel(-48980000, 10000000, 0, 0, 0, 0, 30000, 7, new Color(100, 0, 150));
	    double r_T1B = 1.725;
	    MasseKugel Trappist1B = new MasseKugel(-48980000 - r_T1B, 10000000, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Trappist1.mass * G / r_T1B), 0, 0.85, 4, new Color(200, 50, 50));
	    double r_T1E = 4.395;
	    MasseKugel Trappist1E = new MasseKugel(-48980000 + r_T1E, 10000000, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Trappist1.mass * G / r_T1E), 0, 0.69, 4, new Color(50, 180, 150));
	    double r_T1H = 9.285;
	    MasseKugel Trappist1H = new MasseKugel(-48980000 - r_T1H, 10000000, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(Trappist1.mass * G / r_T1H), 0, 0.33, 3, new Color(150, 150, 255));

	    // Proxima Centauri (~4.2 Lichtjahre entfernt)
	    MasseKugel ProximaCen = new MasseKugel(800*50000, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 41500, 8, new Color(150, 0, 0));
	    double r_ProximaB = 7.275;
	    MasseKugel ProximaB = new MasseKugel(800*50000 + r_ProximaB, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(ProximaCen.mass * G / r_ProximaB), 0, 1.27, 5, new Color(180, 50, 50));
	    double r_ProximaD = 4.328;
	    MasseKugel ProximaD = new MasseKugel(800*50000 - r_ProximaD, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(ProximaCen.mass * G / r_ProximaD), 0, 0.26, 3, new Color(255, 100, 0));

	    // 🔹 NEU: Kepler-186 System (~500 Lichtjahre)
	    MasseKugel Kepler186 = new MasseKugel(-1200*50000, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 179820, 6, new Color(200, 50, 0));
	    double r_K186f = 74.4; // skaliert auf dein System
	    MasseKugel Kepler186f = new MasseKugel(-1200*50000 + r_K186f, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(Kepler186.mass * G / r_K186f), 0, 1.0, 4, new Color(50, 200, 100));

	    // 🔹 NEU: TOI-715 System (~137 Lichtjahre)
	    MasseKugel TOI715 = new MasseKugel(1000*50000, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 76590, 5, new Color(220, 80, 0));
	    double r_TOI715b = 12.1;
	    MasseKugel TOI715b = new MasseKugel(1000*50000 + r_TOI715b, 0, 0, 0, -Math.sqrt(TOI715.mass * G / r_TOI715b), 0, 1.55, 4, new Color(255, 120, 80));
	    double r_TOI715c = 18.3;
	    MasseKugel TOI715c = new MasseKugel(1000*50000 - r_TOI715c, 0, 0, 0, Math.sqrt(TOI715.mass * G / r_TOI715c), 0, 1.05, 4, new Color(255, 160, 100));

	    // 🔹 NEU: LHS 1140 System (~49 Lichtjahre)
	    MasseKugel LHS1140 = new MasseKugel(0, 1000*50000, 0, 0, 0, 0, 59940, 5, new Color(180, 60, 0));
	    double r_LHS1140b = 23.5;
	    MasseKugel LHS1140b = new MasseKugel(0, 1000*50000 + r_LHS1140b, 0, -Math.sqrt(LHS1140.mass * G / r_LHS1140b), 0, 0, 6.8, 5, new Color(100, 220, 180));

	    // Alle Körper hinzufügen
	    bodies.add(Sonne);
	    bodies.add(Merkur); bodies.add(Venus); bodies.add(Erde); bodies.add(Mars);
	    bodies.add(Ceres);
	    bodies.add(Jupiter); bodies.add(Saturn); bodies.add(Uranus); bodies.add(Neptun);
	    bodies.add(Pluto); bodies.add(Eris); bodies.add(Haumea); bodies.add(Makemake);
	    bodies.add(Trappist1); bodies.add(Trappist1B); bodies.add(Trappist1E); bodies.add(Trappist1H);
	    bodies.add(ProximaCen); bodies.add(ProximaB); bodies.add(ProximaD);
	    bodies.add(Kepler186); bodies.add(Kepler186f);
	    bodies.add(TOI715); bodies.add(TOI715b); bodies.add(TOI715c);
	    bodies.add(LHS1140); bodies.add(LHS1140b);
	}

	// unserer Sonne. Bitte führe eine Umfangreiche Analyse auf allen Ebenen durch und korrigiere jegliche

	    // Startet sehr weit entfernt (1000 Einheiten) mit einer hohen Geschwindigkeit,
	    // die größer ist als die Fluchtgeschwindigkeit, damit das Objekt das Sonnensystem wieder verlassen kann.
	    MasseKugel ATLAS_Interstellar = new MasseKugel(1000.0, 1000.0, 0, -38.0, -38.0, 0, 1.0e-12, 1, new Color(50, 200, 255));


	    // Alle Körper hinzufügen
	    bodies.add(Sonne);
	    bodies.add(Merkur); bodies.add(Venus); bodies.add(Erde); bodies.add(Mars);
	    bodies.add(Ceres);

	    // Hinzufügen des interstellaren Objekts
	    bodies.add(ATLAS_Interstellar); 

	    // Die Schleife für die 50 zusätzlichen Sonnen wurde entfernt.
	}

	public void masseKugelBasis1(int number, int size) {

		for (int i = 0; i < number; i++) {
			MasseKugel masseKugel = new MasseKugel(size * Math.random(), size * Math.random(), 0, 0, 0, 0,
					Math.random() / Math.random() / Math.random(), 8, new Color(0, 0, 0));
			masseKugel.rot = 255 - 50 * masseKugel.mass;
			masseKugel.green = 255 - 75 * masseKugel.mass;
			masseKugel.blue = 255 - 100 * masseKugel.mass;
//			masseKugel.update(i);
			bodies.add(masseKugel);

		}

	}

	// --- Methoden zum Auslesen/Speichern der Bodies ---
	public List<MasseKugel> getBodies() {
		return new ArrayList<>(bodies);
	}

	// Methoden für die Geschwindigkeitsanpassung, umbenannt für Klarheit
	public double apspeed = 1; // Simulationsgeschwindigkeit - als Klassenvariable definiert

	public void increaseSimulationSpeed() {
		apspeed *= 1.2;
		repaint();
	}

	public void decreaseSimulationSpeed() {
		apspeed /= 1.2;
		slow = slow / apspeed;
		System.out.println(TIMER_DELAY);
		repaint();
	}

	private void rotateBodyAroundDegrees(MasseKugel body, MasseKugel center, double degrees) {
		double theta = Math.toRadians(degrees);
		rotateBodyAround(body, center, theta);
	}

	private void rotateBodyAround(MasseKugel body, MasseKugel center, double theta) {
		double dx = body.x - center.x;
		double dy = body.y - center.y;
		double cos = Math.cos(theta);
		double sin = Math.sin(theta);
		double newDx = dx * cos - dy * sin;
		double newDy = dx * sin + dy * cos;
		body.x = center.x + newDx;
		body.y = center.y + newDy;
		double vx = body.vx;
		double vy = body.vy;
		body.vx = vx * cos - vy * sin;
		body.vy = vx * sin + vy * cos;
	}

	// NEU: Methode zur Berechnung der kinetischen Gesamtenergie aller Körper
	public double getEKinGes() {
		double EKinGes = 0;
		for (MasseKugel m : bodies) {
			EKinGes += m.getEKin(); // Ruft die Methode getEKin() der MasseKugel auf
		}
		return EKinGes;
	}

	// NEU: Korrigierte Methode zur Berechnung der potentiellen Gesamtenergie
	// Sie summiert die potenzielle Energie zwischen *allen einzigartigen Paaren*
	// von Himmelskörpern.
	public double getEPotGes() {
		double totalEPot = 0;
		for (int i = 0; i < bodies.size(); i++) {
			MasseKugel b1 = bodies.get(i);
			for (int j = i + 1; j < bodies.size(); j++) { // Schleife über einzigartige Paare (j beginnt bei i+1)
				MasseKugel b2 = bodies.get(j);

				double dx = b2.x - b1.x;
				double dy = b2.y - b1.y;
				double dz = b2.z - b1.z; // Berücksichtigt die Z-Koordinate für den Abstand in 3D

				double r = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz);

				// Behandle extrem kleine Abstände, um Division durch Null oder sehr große Werte
				// zu vermeiden
				// Schwellenwert (0.001) kann bei Bedarf an die Simulationsskala angepasst
				// werden
				if (r < 0.001) {
					r = 0.001;
				}

				totalEPot += -G * b1.mass * b2.mass / r;
			}
		}
		return totalEPot;
	}

	// Die ursprüngliche getEPot(MasseKugel m)-Methode wurde entfernt,
	// da sie nicht für die paarweise Berechnung der potenziellen Energie in einem
	// N-Körper-System geeignet war.
	/*
	 * public double getEPot(MasseKugel m) { double EKin=
	 * -G*m.mass*getGesMass()/m.getDistZero(); return EKin; }
	 */

	public double getGesMass() {
		double gesMass = 0;
		for (MasseKugel m : bodies) {
			gesMass += m.mass;
		}
		return gesMass;
	}

	public void masseKugelBasis(double x, double y, double z, int anzahl) {
		for (int i = 0; i < anzahl; i++) {
			MasseKugel mk = new MasseKugel(Math.random() * x, Math.random() * y, Math.random() * z, 0, 0, 0, 1, 8,
					Color.LIGHT_GRAY);
			bodies.add(mk);
		}
	}

	public void masseKugelBasis2(int number, int size, int speed) {
		for (int i = 0; i < number; i++) {
			MasseKugel mk = new MasseKugel(Math.random() * size-Math.random() * size, Math.random() * size-Math.random() * size, Math.random() * size-Math.random() * size, Math.random()*speed-Math.random()*speed, Math.random()*speed-Math.random()*speed, Math.random()*speed-Math.random()*speed,
					mass*Math.random()/Math.random(), 8, new Color((int)(Math.random()*256),(int)(Math.random()*256),(int)(Math.random()*256)));
			mk.Ex=energie*Math.random()-energie*Math.random();
			mk.Ey=energie*Math.random()-energie*Math.random();
			mk.Ez=energie*Math.random()-energie*Math.random();
			mk.energie=energie*Math.random()-energie*Math.random();
			bodies.add(mk);
//			mk.rot=mk.color.getRed();
//			mk.green=mk.color.getGreen();
//			mk.blue=mk.color.getBlue();
		}
	}
	
	public void masseKugelBasis7(int dimensionen) {
		for (int i = 0; i < dimensionen; i++) {
			MasseKugel mk = new MasseKugel(Math.random() * size, Math.random() * size, Math.random() * size, 0, 0, 0,
					mass*Math.random()/Math.random(), 8, new Color((int)(Math.random()*256),(int)(Math.random()*256),(int)(Math.random()*256)));
			if(i%(dimensionen/2)==0) {
			if(i%2==0)mk.Ex=100000000.0;
			if(i%2==1)mk.Ex=-100000000.0;}
			if(i%(dimensionen/2)==1) {
				if(i%2==0)mk.Ey=100000000.0;
				if(i%2==1)mk.Ey=-100000000.0;}
			if(i%(dimensionen/2)==2) {
				if(i%2==0)mk.Ez=100000000.0;
				if(i%2==1)mk.Ez=-100000000.0;}
			bodies.add(mk);
//			mk.rot=mk.color.getRed();
//			mk.green=mk.color.getGreen();
//			mk.blue=mk.color.getBlue();
		}
	}

	// --- Pan-Methoden ---
	public void panLeft() {
		zoomCenterX += PAN_STEP;
		repaint();
	}

	public void panRight() {
		zoomCenterX -= PAN_STEP;
		repaint();
	}

	public void panUp() {
		zoomCenterY += PAN_STEP;
		repaint();
	}

	public void panDown() {
		zoomCenterY -= PAN_STEP;
		repaint();
	}

	public void timeUp() {
		time *= 1.5;
	}

	public void timeDown() {
		time /= 1.5;
	}

	// Gelogene Methode
	@Override
	protected void paintComponent(Graphics g) {
		super.paintComponent(g);
		Graphics2D g2 = (Graphics2D) g;
		g2.setColor(Color.BLACK);
		g2.fillRect(0, 0, getWidth(), getHeight());
		for (MasseKugel body : bodies) {
			// Berücksichtige Pan und Zoom bei der Positionierung
			double sx = (zoomCenterX + body.x) * zoomFactor + getWidth() / 2.0;
			double sy = (zoomCenterY + body.y) * zoomFactor + getHeight() / 2.0;
//			int r = (int) Math.max(body.radius * zoomFactor, MIN_RADIUS_DRAW);
			g2.setColor(body.color);
			g2.fillOval((int) (sx - body.radius), (int) (sy - body.radius), body.radius * 2, body.radius * 2);
		}
	}

	void entropieangleichRaum(MasseKugel mp1, MasseKugel mp2) {
		double flow1x = mp1.x * Math.random();
		double flow2x = mp2.x * Math.random();
		mp1.x -= flow1x;
		mp1.x += flow2x;
		mp2.x -= flow2x;
		mp2.x += flow1x;

		double flow1y = mp1.y * Math.random();
		double flow2y = mp2.y * Math.random();
		mp1.y -= flow1x;
		mp1.y += flow2x;
		mp2.y -= flow2x;
		mp2.y += flow1x;

		double flow1z = mp1.z * Math.random();
		double flow2z = mp2.z * Math.random();
		mp1.z -= flow1x;
		mp1.z += flow2x;
		mp2.z -= flow2x;
		mp2.z += flow1x;
	}

	void entropieangleichRaumStep(MasseKugel mp1, MasseKugel mp2) {
		double flow1x = (mp2.x - mp1.x) * Math.random();

		mp1.x += flow1x;
		mp2.x -= flow1x;

		double flow1y = (mp2.y - mp1.y) * Math.random();

		mp1.y += flow1y;
		mp2.y -= flow1y;

		double flow1z = (mp2.z - mp1.z) * Math.random();

		mp1.z += flow1z;
		mp2.z -= flow1z;

	}

	void entropieeichSpeed(MasseKugel mp1, MasseKugel mp2) {
		double flow1x = mp1.vx * Math.random();
		double flow2x = mp2.vx * Math.random();
		mp1.vx -= flow1x;
		mp1.vx += flow2x;
		mp2.vx -= flow2x;
		mp2.vx += flow1x;

		double flow1y = mp1.vy * Math.random();
		double flow2y = mp2.vy * Math.random();
		mp1.vy -= flow1x;
		mp1.vy += flow2x;
		mp2.vy -= flow2x;
		mp2.vy += flow1x;

		double flow1z = mp1.z * Math.random();
		double flow2z = mp2.z * Math.random();
		mp1.vz -= flow1x;
		mp1.vz += flow2x;
		mp2.vz -= flow2x;
		mp2.vz += flow1x;
	}

	public void EntrophieGravity(int verknüpfungen) {
		int n = bodies.size();

		List<MasseKugel> parallelliste1 = new ArrayList<MasseKugel>();
		List<MasseKugel> parallelliste2 = new ArrayList<MasseKugel>();
		List<MasseKugel> parallelliste3 = new ArrayList<MasseKugel>();
		List<MasseKugel> parallelliste4 = new ArrayList<MasseKugel>();
		List<MasseKugel> parallelliste5 = new ArrayList<MasseKugel>();
		List<MasseKugel> parallelliste6 = new ArrayList<MasseKugel>();

		for (int z = 0; z < bodies.size(); z++) {

			parallelliste1.add(bodies.get((int) (bodies.size() * Math.random())));
			parallelliste2.add(bodies.get((int) (bodies.size() * Math.random())));
			parallelliste3.add(bodies.get((int) (bodies.size() * Math.random())));
			parallelliste4.add(bodies.get((int) (bodies.size() * Math.random())));
			parallelliste5.add(bodies.get((int) (bodies.size() * Math.random())));
			parallelliste6.add(bodies.get((int) (bodies.size() * Math.random())));
//				parallelliste1.add(bodies.get((int) (bodies.size()*Math.random())));

		}

		int i = (int) (Math.random() * n);
		double[] mins = new double[verknüpfungen];
		for (int j = 0; j < verknüpfungen; j++) {
			MasseKugel mi = bodies.get(i);
			if (i + 1 < n) {
				MasseKugel mj = bodies.get(i + 1);

				double dx = mj.x - mi.x;
				double dy = mj.y - mi.y;
				double dz = mj.z - mi.z;

				double r2 = dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz;
				double r = Math.sqrt(r2);

				entropieangleichRaumStep(mi, mj);
			}

			if (i - 1 >= n) {
				MasseKugel mj = bodies.get(i - 1);

				double dx = mj.x - mi.x;
				double dy = mj.y - mi.y;
				double dz = mj.z - mi.z;

				double r2 = dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz;
				double r = Math.sqrt(r2);

				entropieangleichRaumStep(mi, mj);
			}
			if (verknüpfungen > 2) {
				MasseKugel mj = parallelliste1.get(i);
				double dx = mj.x - mi.x;
				double dy = mj.y - mi.y;
				double dz = mj.z - mi.z;
				double r2 = dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz;
				double r = Math.sqrt(r2);
				entropieangleichRaumStep(mi, mj);
			}

			if (verknüpfungen > 3) {
				MasseKugel mj = parallelliste1.get(i);
				double dx = mj.x - mi.x;
				double dy = mj.y - mi.y;
				double dz = mj.z - mi.z;
				double r2 = dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz;
				double r = Math.sqrt(r2);
				entropieangleichRaumStep(mi, mj);
			}

		}
	}

	public void GravityStochastisch() {
		int n = bodies.size();

		// 1. Zufällige Auswahl von zwei verschiedenen Körpern (Input-Phase)
		if (n < 2)
			return; // Abbruch, wenn zu wenige Körper vorhanden sind

		int i = (int) (Math.random() * n);
		int j;
		do {
			j = (int) (Math.random() * n);
		} while (i == j); // Stelle sicher, dass i und j verschieden sind

		MasseKugel bi = bodies.get(i);
		MasseKugel bj = bodies.get(j);

		// Wir iterieren nicht über alle Kugeln, sondern nur über dieses Paar.

		// 2. Berechnung der Beschleunigung (Operation)
		double dx = bj.x - bi.x;
		double dy = bj.y - bi.y;
		double dz = bj.z - bi.z;

		double r2 = dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz;
		double r = Math.sqrt(r2);

		// Kollisionsschutz (numerische Stabilität)
		if (r < 1e-3)
			r = 1e-3;

		// Beschleunigung, die Körper 'bi' erfährt: a_i = G * m_j / r^2
		double a_i = G * bj.mass / r2;

		// Beschleunigung, die Körper 'bj' erfährt: a_j = G * m_i / r^2
		double a_j = G * bi.mass / r2;

		// 3. Geschwindigkeits-Updates für BEIDE Körper (Output-Phase)
		// bi.vx += a_i * Zeit * Richtung
		if (bi.movable) {
			bi.vx += (a_i * dx / r) * time;
			bi.vy += (a_i * dy / r) * time;
			bi.vz += (a_i * dz / r) * time;
		}

		// bj.vx -= a_j * Zeit * Richtung (Richtung umgekehrt, daher -)
		if (bj.movable) {
			// Achtung: bj beschleunigt in Richtung -dx, -dy, -dz
			bj.vx -= (a_j * dx / r) * time;
			bj.vy -= (a_j * dy / r) * time;
			bj.vz -= (a_j * dz / r) * time;
		}

		// 4. Positions-Updates für BEIDE Körper (mit der nun korrigierten
		// Geschwindigkeit)
		bi.updatePosition(time);
		bj.updatePosition(time);

		// WICHTIG: repaint muss im ActionPerformed-Loop aufgerufen werden,
		// außerhalb dieser Gravity-Methode.
	}

	// Gravity für 3D Raum
	public void Gravity() {
		int n = bodies.size();
		double[] ax = new double[n];
		double[] ay = new double[n];
		double[] az = new double[n];

		for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
			MasseKugel bi = bodies.get(i);
			ax[i] = ay[i] = az[i] = 0;
			if (!bi.movable)
				continue;
			for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
				if (i == j)
					continue;
				MasseKugel bj = bodies.get(j);
				double dx = bj.x - bi.x;
				double dy = bj.y - bi.y;
				double dz = bj.z - bi.z;

				double r2 = dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz;
				double r = Math.sqrt(r2);

				double normdx = dx / r;
				double normdy = dy / r;
				double normdz = dz / r;

				bi.vx += G * bj.mass * normdx / Math.pow(r, 2);
				bi.vy += G * bj.mass * normdy / Math.pow(r, 2);
				bi.vz += G * bj.mass * normdz / Math.pow(r, 2);
			}
		}
	}

	public void Gravity(int verknüpfungen) {
		int n = bodies.size();

		for (int i = 0; i < n*2-2; i+=2) {
			
			MasseKugel bi = bodies.get(i/2);
			MasseKugel bj = bodies.get(i/2+1);

			if (bi == bj)
				continue;
			double dx = bj.x - bi.x;
			double dy = bj.y - bi.y;
			double dz = bj.z - bi.z;
			double r2 = dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz;
			double r = Math.sqrt(r2);

			double f = G * bi.mass * bj.mass / r / r;
			// f=m*a
			// abi=f/bi.mass
			double abi = f / bi.mass;
			double abj = f / bj.mass;
//				double a = G * bj.mass / r2;
			bi.vx += (abi * dx / r * time*0.5);
			bi.vy += (abi * dy / r * time*0.5);
			bi.vz += (abi * dz / r * time*0.5);

			bj.vx -= (abj * dx / r * time*0.5);
			bj.vy -= (abj * dy / r * time*0.5);
			bj.vz -= (abj * dz / r * time*0.5);
			bi.updatePosition(time/n);
			bj.updatePosition(time/n);
		}

		// double array mit Geschwindigkeitswerten zu verknüpfungen/2 Raumdimensionen

		
		repaint();

	}
	
	public void entrophy(double d) {
		for(int i=0; i<d; i++) {
			MasseKugel m= bodies.get((int)(bodies.size()*Math.random()));
			m.randomUpdatePosition();
		}
	}
	
	public void colorEntrophy(double d) {
		for(int i=0; i<d; i++) {
			MasseKugel m= bodies.get((int)(bodies.size()*Math.random()));
			m.updateColor();
			m.randomUpdatePositionColor();
			m.randomSpeedColor();
		}
	}
	
	public void massEntrophy(double d) {
		for(int i=0; i<d; i++) {
			double richtung=Math.random();
			int random=(int)(bodies.size()*Math.random());
			MasseKugel m= bodies.get(random);
		
			
			MasseKugel m2= bodies.get(random);
			if(richtung>0.5&&random<bodies.size()-1) m2= bodies.get(random+1);
			if(richtung>0.5&&random==bodies.size()-1) {m2= new MasseKugel(size*random/random,size*random/random,size*random/random,size*random/random,size*random/random,size*random/random,this.mass*random/random,7,new Color(10,0,0));
			m2.rot=Math.random()*255-Math.random()*255;
			m2.green=Math.random()*255-Math.random()*255;
			m2.blue=Math.random()*255-Math.random()*255;
			bodies.add(m2);}
			if(richtung<=0.5&&random>0) m2= bodies.get(random-1);
			
			
			
			
			double mass=Math.abs(m.mass-m2.mass)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random();
			
//			double x =(m.x-m2.x)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.1;
//			double y =(m.y-m2.y)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.1;
//			double z =(m.z-m2.z)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.1;
			double vx =(m.vx-m2.vx)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.1;
			double vy =(m.vy-m2.vy)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.1;
			double vz =(m.vz-m2.vz)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.1;
			double Ex =(m.Ex-m2.Ex)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.5;
			double Ey =(m.Ey-m2.Ey)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.5;
			double Ez =(m.Ez-m2.Ez)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.5;
			double Ekin =(m.EKin-m2.EKin)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random()*0.7;
		
			
			double rot =(m.rot-m2.rot)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random();
			double green =(m.green-m2.green)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random();
			double blue =(m.blue-m2.blue)*Math.random()*Math.random()*Math.random();
			
			
			
			m.mass-=mass;
			m2.mass+=mass;
//			m.x-=x;
//			m2.x+=x;
//			m.y-=y;
//			m2.y+=y;
//			m.z-=z;
//			m2.z+=z;
			
			
			m.vx-=vx;
			m2.vx+=vx;
			m.vy-=vy;
			m2.vy+=vy;
			m.vz-=vz;
			m2.vz+=vz;
			
			m.rot-=rot;
			m2.rot+=rot;
			m.green-=green;
			m2.green-=green;
			m.blue-=blue;
			m2.blue+=blue;
			
			m.Ex-=Ex;
			m2.Ex+=Ex;
			m.Ey-=Ey;
			m2.Ey+=Ey;
			m.Ez-=Ez;
			m2.Ez+=Ez;
			m.EKin-=Ekin;
			m2.EKin+=Ekin;
			
		
			
//			m.x-=x;
//			m2.x+=x;
//			m.y-=y;
//			m2.y+=y;
//			m.z-=z;
//			m2.z+=z;
			
			
			
			
			m.updateColor();
			m2.updateColor();
			
			
			
//			m.randomUpdatePositionColor();
//			m2.randomUpdatePositionColor();
			
			m.updateColor();
			m2.updateColor();
			
//			m.randomUpdateSpeed();
//			m2.randomUpdateSpeed();
			
			m.randomUpdateE();
			m2.randomUpdateE();
			
			m.randomUpdatePositionv();
			m2.randomUpdatePositionv();
			
			
		}
	}
	
	public void entropieNeu(int steps) {

			mk1.updateColor();
			mk2.updateColor();}
		
		}
//			else {

////			if(Math.random()>0.9)mk1.entropieOther2(mk2);
////			if(Math.random()>0.9)mk1.entropieOther(mk2);

double gravityGeminiConter=0;
	public void GravityGemini() {
		gravityGeminiConter++;
		for (int i2 = 0; i2 < steps; i2++) {
			int n = bodies.size();
			double[] ax = new double[n];
			double[] ay = new double[n];
			double[] az = new double[n];
			for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
				MasseKugel bi = bodies.get(i);
				ax[i] = ay[i] = az[i] = 0;
				if (!bi.movable)
					continue;
				for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
					if (i == j)
						continue;
					MasseKugel bj = bodies.get(j);
					double dx = bj.x - bi.x;
					double dy = bj.y - bi.y;
					double dz = bj.z - bi.z;
					double r2 = dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz;
					double r = Math.sqrt(r2);
					double a = G * bj.mass / r2;
					ax[i] += a * dx / r;
					ay[i] += a * dy / r;
					az[i] += a * dz / r;
				}
			}
			for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
				MasseKugel b = bodies.get(i);
				if (b.movable) {
					b.vx += (ax[i] * time);
					b.vy += (ay[i] * time);
					b.vz += (az[i] * time);
//					b.y+=(ay[i]*Math.random()*time-ay[i]*Math.random()*time);
				}
				
				
//				if(Math.random()>0.9999)b.entropieMasse();
//				b.updateColor();
				
				b.updatePosition(time);
				
				
				 
				
			}
		}
		repaint();
	}

	// Zoom-Funktionen
	public void zoomIn() {
		zoomFactor *= ZOOM_STEP;
		PAN_STEP = feinheit / zoomFactor;
		repaint();
	}

	public void zoomOut() {
		zoomFactor /= ZOOM_STEP;
		PAN_STEP = feinheit / zoomFactor;
		repaint();
	}

	public static void main(String[] args) {
		System.out.println("public static void main(String[] args) {");

public class MasseKugel {

	public double basisEntroDouble;

	public double EKin;
	public double Ex;
